    <div hidden id="doc-title">Exotic Goods in Headsmen</div>

  <p> Exotica curator: <strong>Isoard of Devilville</strong>.  He has short blonde hair, wild green eyes and elegant posture (<em>Calm</em>). <small>In the pocket: <strong>a deck of cards</strong> and <strong>a magnifying glass</strong>.</small>  <ul>        <li> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('cg5azHw2');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> Twice a year, Isoard will want to <strong>acquire exotic artifacts</strong> in <a href="/sandbox/nTR8nJOW/hex/Y6B8cHbe"><strong>Black Shield Timberlands</strong> (hex E5S29)</a> and will look for someone to protect him throughout the journey. </li>   <li class="inactive-quest"> Unlock this page and click here <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll_ex('kDNxqz4N','RerollerQuest');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> for a hook </li>   </ul> </p> <p>  <h5> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll_ex('JmrQnDsv','ExoticGoodsInventory');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> Inventory </h5> <table><tr><th>Item</th><th>Price</th </tr>   <tr> <td>Glowworm</td> <td>1 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Phosphorescent Moss</td> <td>1 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Ruby (as dust)</td> <td>55 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Crystal Vial of phosphorescent material</td> <td>22 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Sacrificial Offering appropriate to deity</td> <td>28 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Jade Circlet</td> <td>1,650 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Diamond (as dust)</td> <td>28 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Alum soaked in vinegar</td> <td>6 cp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Ivory Portal (miniature)</td> <td>6 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Mercury</td> <td>6 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Diamonds</td> <td>330 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Crystal Bead</td> <td>6 sp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Fur of Bat</td> <td>2 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Snaketongue</td> <td>1 cp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Wire of fine silver</td> <td>1 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Diamond and Opal, powdered mix</td> <td>1,100 gp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Feather</td> <td>1 sp</td> </tr>  <tr> <td>Makeup</td> <td>1 gp</td> </tr>  </table>  </p>
